## [1.33.2](https://bitbucket.org/centraltechnology/centech-api/compare/versions/1.33.1...versions/1.33.2) (2020-03-12)

### Breaking Changes

- `mutation addCustomerAddress, editCustomerAddress` now return `CustomerAddress`

#### `type CustomerAddress` [See diff](https://bitbucket.org/centraltechnology/centech-api/pull-requests/219/refactor-customer-address#chg-packages/api/src/schema/customer/customerSchema.graphql)

- move `building`, `address_name`, `address_line`, `branch_id`, `customer_address_type`, `full_tax_type` out of `custom_attributes`
- field `city`, `street` is deprecated and default to `n/a`
- field `region`, `region_id` is deprecated, use `province` instead
- field `district`, `district_id` is group to `district` and move out of `custom_attributes`
- field `subdistrict`, `subdistrict_id` is group to `subdistrict` and move out of `custom_attributes`
- field `default_shipping`, `default_billing` is deprecated. use `is_default_shipping` and `is_default_billing` instead
- field `customer_address_type` change from `String` to `enum AddressType`
- field `full_tax_type` change from `String` to `enum TaxType`


#### `type CreateCustomerAddress` [See diff](https://bitbucket.org/centraltechnology/centech-api/pull-requests/219/refactor-customer-address#chg-packages/api/src/schema/address/addressSchema.graphql)

- same as `type CustomerAddress`
- required `firstname`, `lastname`, `telephone`, `address_line`, `subdistrict`, `district`, `province`, `postcode`, `customer_address_type`

#### `type EditCustomerAddress` [See diff](https://bitbucket.org/centraltechnology/centech-api/pull-requests/219/refactor-customer-address#chg-packages/api/src/schema/address/addressSchema.graphql)

- same as `type CustomerAddress`
- required only `id`, `subdistrict`, `district`, `customer_address_type`
